Lot of people saying TENET is &quot;confusing&quot;.  Well, it&#39;s on HBO Max now, and I&#39;ve watched it, and it only took one viewing to convince me that people just don&#39;t pay attention during movies.  Without giving away any spoilers, I can tell you that <b>TENET</b> tells you, repeatedly, what&#39;s going on during the movie.  Where most movies would devote dialogue to the characters and their backstories and motivations and relationships with each other, TENET reserves its speaky moments for explaining things that are about to happen; and then, explaining things that <b>are</b> happening; and then, explaining things that <b>just</b> happened.  If you can&#39;t understand what&#39;s happening in TENET, that&#39;s not the movie&#39;s fault.  It did everything it could to explain it to you.  And honestly, it&#39;s not even that hard to understand.  A little technobabble here and there, and the overarching explanation that some things are just plain happening backwards.  That&#39;s really all you need to know.

Honestly, i wanted to watch this trailer today just to feel this magic again, because the whole film felt like a big trailer, like a daydream. This film is on the wonderland level of Stalker or Eraserhead. When you are in a dream, it all makes perfect sense, but try to recall the plot, or logic awoken and it all crumbles down like a house of cards. We need more of those insightful dreams and not commercialised meaningless word scribbles. Some say that dreams are meaningless, but than why so many religious texts rely on dreams and hallucinations? Best stories were written by the people who often daydreamed, so let your brain tell you more incredible stories. Dream and explore your mind, friends.

Inside Freeport, they find a machine (later referred to as &quot;Turnstile&quot;) from which two masked men emerge; the inverted one attacks the Protagonist, while Neil chases after the normal one, whom he manages to unmask. Great cast , great action , good concept but the story is an absolute mess
Christopher nolan is the most over rated story teller of all time... people think his films are super complex but really he&#39;s just very bad at creating and telling a story. His characters are 1 dimensional, his writing is boring and flat, and his story archs are painfully forced and plastic. His latest turd seals the deal for me- tenet... oh my fucking god, what an abysmally shallow mess. I believe his thinking went something like this- &quot;i wanna film forwards motion alongside backwards motion, that would look super sick and epic&quot;, and he forced a really REALLY boring story driven by flat characters with zero development and terrible dialogue which is drowned out by A TOTALLY EPIC SCORE around that model and ended up with tenet, a film with so many plotholes you have to just say &quot;ok, so this this is 100% just a visual spectacle, don&#39;t look any deeper than that&quot;.
